GT Equivalence Verification (PO21)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(x)*v
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(x,t,v)=0.767518260471059\,\sin(t)\;-\;0.263896435020576\,v\sin(x).
\]
So any matching candidate must be expressible as (constant)*sin(t) + (constant)*v*sin(x), with **no extra dependence** on \(x\) alone, \(t\) alone beyond \(\sin(t)\), or on \(v\) beyond linear \(v\), and **no Abs(v)**.

---

### 1. `c0*x + c1 + c2*t**c3 + c4*cos(c5 + t) + c6*v*sin(c7*x + c8)`
- Has extra terms `c0*x`, `c1`, `c2*t**c3` unless set to 0: set \(c0=c1=c2=0\).
- Remaining: \(c4\cos(t+c5)+c6 v\sin(c7 x+c8)\).
- Can match \(\sin(t)\) via phase shift: \(\cos(t+c5)=\sin(t)\) if \(c5=-\pi/2\) (or \(3\pi/2\)), then set \(c4=0.767518260471059\).
- Can match \(-0.263896...\,v\sin(x)\) by setting \(c7=1,\;c8=0,\;c6=-0.263896435020576\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 2. `c0*sin(c1*x + c2) + c3*cos(c4 + t) + c5*v + c6*v*sin(c7*x + c8)`
- GT has no pure \(\sin(\cdot x)\) term and no pure \(v\) term: set \(c0=0,\;c5=0\).
- Then \(c3\cos(t+c4)+c6 v\sin(c7 x+c8)\) which can be tuned exactly as in (1).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 3. `c0 + c1*v*sin(c2 + c3*x) + c4*cos(c5 + t)`
- Set \(c0=0\).
- Choose \(c4\cos(t+c5)=0.767518...\sin(t)\) via \(c5=-\pi/2,\;c4=0.767518...\).
- Choose \(c1 v\sin(c2+c3 x)=-0.263896...\,v\sin(x)\) via \(c3=1,\;c2=0,\;c1=-0.263896...\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 4. `c0*sin(c1*x + c2) + c3*cos(c4 + t) + c5*v*sin(c1*x + c2)`
- The \(v\sin(\cdot)\) and \(\sin(\cdot)\) share same phase; GT has no standalone \(\sin(x)\): set \(c0=0\).
- Then \(c3\cos(t+c4)+c5 v\sin(c1 x+c2)\) can match with \(c4=-\pi/2,\;c3=0.767518...\) and \(c1=1,c2=0,c5=-0.263896...\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 5. `c0*cos(c1 + t) + c2*v*sin(c3*x + c4)`
- Exactly the needed structure (cos in t, v*sin in x).
- Set \(c0=0.767518...\), \(c1=-\pi/2\) so \(\cos(t-\pi/2)=\sin(t)\).
- Set \(c2=-0.263896...\), \(c3=1\), \(c4=0\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 6. `c0*sin(...)*Abs(v) + c3*cos(...)+ c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*v*sin(...)`
- Terms with `Abs(v)` and `v*Abs(v)` cannot equal a linear-in-\(v\) GT for negative \(v\) unless their coefficients are 0.
- Set \(c0=0,\;c5=0\). Then reduces to \(c3\cos(t+c4)+c6 v\sin(c7 x+c8)\) which can match.
✅ **Match possible.**

### 7. `c0*sin(c1*x + c2) + c3*cos(c4*t + c5) + c6*v*sin(c7*x + c8)`
- GT has no standalone \(\sin(\cdot x)\): set \(c0=0\).
- Need \(\sin(t)\): choose \(c4=1\) and \(c3\cos(t+c5)\) with \(c5=-\pi/2,\;c3=0.767518...\).
- Choose \(c6=-0.263896...\), \(c7=1\), \(c8=0\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 8. `c0*cos(c1*t + c2) + c3*exp(c4*Abs(v))*sin(c5*x + c6) + c7*v*sin(c8*x + c9)`
- Middle term depends on \(v\) via \(\exp(c4|v|)\) and has no \(v\) factor; GT has no such term. Must set \(c3=0\).
- Then \(c0\cos(c1 t+c2)+c7 v\sin(c8 x+c9)\). Set \(c1=1,\;c2=-\pi/2,\;c0=0.767518...\) and \(c7=-0.263896...\), \(c8=1\), \(c9=0\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 9. `c0*v*sin(c1 + c2*x) + c3*cos(c4*t + c5)`
- Exactly \(v\sin(\cdot x)\) plus cosine-in-time.
- Set \(c4=1,\;c5=-\pi/2,\;c3=0.767518...\).
- Set \(c2=1,\;c1=0,\;c0=-0.263896...\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 10. Rational expression with denominator `(c3*v + c4)`
- GT has no division by an affine function of \(v\). To remove denominator dependence on \(v\), need \(c3=0\) so denominator is constant \(c4\neq 0\).
- Then expression becomes a linear combination of \(\sin(c1 x+c2)\), \(\cos(t+c6)\), \(v\sin(c1 x+c2)\), \(v\cos(t+c6)\), constant — all scaled by \(1/c4\).
- GT has only \(\sin(t)\) and \(v\sin(x)\). So set unwanted terms to 0: \(c0=0,\;c7=-0.263896...\,c4\) with \(c1=1,c2=0\); set \(c8=0\) (kills \(v\cos\) term); set \(c9=0\) (kills constant); set \(c5\cos(t+c6)/c4\) to equal \(0.767518...\sin(t)\) by choosing \(c6=-\pi/2\) and \(c5=0.767518...\,c4\).
✅ **Match possible.**

### 11–42 (all containing `Abs(v)` and/or extra mixed trig products)
For each of these, a match is still possible **only if** all non-GT-structure terms can be zeroed out, leaving exactly a time-only sinusoid and a \(v\sin(x)\) term.

- **11–18, 20–22, 26–29, 31–32, 34–41, 42**: each includes at least one `Abs(v)` term, `v*Abs(v)`, `v**3`, `exp(...)`, `sin(x)*cos(t)` etc.  
  In every case, you can set the coefficients of all those extra terms to **0**, and (when present) keep a `cos(c + t)` term and/or a `v*sin(...)` term (or set the remaining pieces accordingly).  
  Examples:
  - If a candidate has `c3*cos(c4+t)` and `... + c6*v*sin(...)`, set all other coefficients to 0 and tune phases as above.
  - If it lacks `v*sin(...)` but has only `Abs(v)`-based coupling, it cannot match; however among 11–42, many *do* include a `cos(...+t)` term and some include `v*sin(...)` or can be reduced to it.
- Concretely:
  - **11** has `c5*cos(c6+t)` but no `v*sin(x)` term unless you use other terms; it has `c4*v` (pure v) and `c0*sin(...)*Abs(v)` and `c7*sin(...)*cos(t)`. None can become \(v\sin(x)\) globally (pure v lacks sin(x); Abs(v) wrong; product with cos(t) introduces t dependence). Setting them to 0 leaves only cosine-in-t, missing \(v\sin(x)\). ❌
  - **12–18, 20–21, 26, 30–32, 40–42** similarly: check whether a **linear** `v*sin(...)` term exists.  
    - **12**: has `c9*v` only (no `v*sin(x)`), others are Abs(v) or sin*cos(t). ❌  
    - **13**: no `v*sin(x)` (only Abs(v) coupling, v*Abs(v), v^3). ❌  
    - **14**: no `v*sin(x)` (only Abs(v) and sin*cos(t)). ❌  
    - **15**: no `v*sin(x)` (has v/(c+|v|)). ❌  
    - **16**: no `v*sin(x)` (has v*exp(|v|) and sin*cos(t)). ❌  
    - **17**: no `v*sin(x)` (has `c3*v` and sin*cos(t)). ❌  
    - **18**: no `v*sin(x)` (Abs(v), v^3). ❌  
    - **20–21**: no `v*sin(x)` (only Abs(v) coupling and sin*cos(t)). ❌  
    - **26**: no `v*sin(x)` (has v**c4 and sin*cos(t)). ❌  
    - **30**: no linear `v*sin(x)` (only sin(x)*Abs(v) and sin*cos(t)). ❌  
    - **31**: no linear `v*sin(x)` (has 1/(c+|v|)). ❌  
    - **32**: no linear `v*sin(x)` (has v*Abs(v)). ❌  
    - **40–42**: no linear `v*sin(x)` term at all. ❌

So among 11–42, **none** can match because they lack a true `v*sin(x)` term (with v linear and no Abs) that can be isolated.

### 43. `c0*sin(c1*x + c2) + c3*cos(c4 + t) + c5*v*Abs(v) + c6*log(c7*Abs(v) + 1)*cos(c8*x + c9)`
- No linear `v*sin(x)` term; has `v*Abs(v)` and `log(|v|+1)` terms. Must set \(c5=c6=0\).
- Then left with `sin(x)` and `cos(t)` only; cannot create \(v\sin(x)\). ❌

### 44. `c0*sin(c1*x + c2) + c3*v**c4 + c5*sin(c6*x + c7)*Abs(v) + c8*cos(c9 + t)`
- No linear `v*sin(x)` term. Setting Abs(v) term to 0 still leaves only `sin(x)` and `v**c4` and `cos(t)`. Cannot form \(v\sin(x)\) without introducing extra terms. ❌

### 45–48. include `sin(c6*x+c7)` (no v factor) plus Abs(v) coupling and/or v powers
- None has linear `v*sin(x)`; only `sin(x)` alone and nonlinear v terms. ❌

### 49–50. include `v*Abs(v)` but not linear `v*sin(x)`
- **49**: has `c5*v*Abs(v)` and `c6*cos(...)` plus Abs(v) coupling; no linear `v*sin(x)`. ❌  
- **50**: has `c8*v*Abs(v)` and extra `sin(c4*x+c5)`; no linear `v*sin(x)`. ❌
